3373    // i32 atomic Add with i32
3374    fn i32_atomic_add(
3375        &mut self,
3376        loc: Location,
3377        target: Location,
3378        memarg: &MemArg,
3379        ret: Location,
3380        need_check: bool,
3381        imported_memories: bool,
3382        offset: i32,
3383        heap_access_oob: Label,
3384        unaligned_atomic: Label,
3385    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
3386        self.memory_op(
3387            target,
3388            memarg,
3389            true,
3390            4,
3391            need_check,
3392            imported_memories,
3393            offset,
3394            heap_access_oob,
3395            unaligned_atomic,
3396            |this, addr| {
3397                let mut temps = vec![];
3398                let tmp1 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
3399                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
3400                })?;
3401                let tmp2 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
3402                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
3403                })?;
3404                let dst =
3405                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
3406                let reread = this.get_label();
3407
3408                this.emit_label(reread)?;
3409                this.assembler
3410                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S32, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
3411                this.emit_binop_add32(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
3412                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
3413                    Size::S32,
3414                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
3415                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
3416                    Location::GPR(addr),
3417                )?;
3418                this.assembler
3419                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
3420                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
3421
3422                if dst != ret {
3423                    this.move_location(Size::S32, ret, dst)?;
3424                }
3425                for r in temps {
3426                    this.release_gpr(r);
3427                }
3428                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
3429                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
3430                Ok(())
3431            },
3432        )
3433    }

3653                this.assembler
3654                    .emit_ldaxrb(Size::S32, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
3655                this.emit_binop_sub32(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
3656                this.assembler.emit_stlxrb(
3657                    Size::S32,
3658                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
3659                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
3660                    Location::GPR(addr),
3661                )?;
3662                this.assembler
3663                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
3664                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
3665
3666                if dst != ret {
3667                    this.move_location(Size::S32, ret, dst)?;
3668                }
3669                for r in temps {
3670                    this.release_gpr(r);
3671                }
3672                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
3673                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
3674                Ok(())
3675            },
3676        )
3677    }

4294        ret: Location,
4295        need_check: bool,
4296        imported_memories: bool,
4297        offset: i32,
4298        heap_access_oob: Label,
4299        unaligned_atomic: Label,
4300    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4301        self.memory_op(
4302            target,
4303            memarg,
4304            true,
4305            4,
4306            need_check,
4307            imported_memories,
4308            offset,
4309            heap_access_oob,
4310            unaligned_atomic,
4311            |this, addr| {
4312                let mut temps = vec![];
4313                let tmp = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
4314                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
4315                })?;
4316                let dst =
4317                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4318                let org =
4319                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4320                let reread = this.get_label();
4321
4322                this.emit_label(reread)?;
4323                this.assembler
4324                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S32, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
4325                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
4326                    Size::S32,
4327                    Location::GPR(tmp),
4328                    org,
4329                    Location::GPR(addr),
4330                )?;
4331                this.assembler
4332                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), reread)?;
4333                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
4334
4335                if dst != ret {
4336                    this.move_location(Size::S32, ret, dst)?;
4337                }
4338                for r in temps {
4339                    this.release_gpr(r);
4340                }
4341                this.release_gpr(tmp);
4342                Ok(())
4343            },
4344        )
4345    }

4462    // i32 atomic Exchange with i32
4463    fn i32_atomic_cmpxchg(
4464        &mut self,
4465        new: Location,
4466        cmp: Location,
4467        target: Location,
4468        memarg: &MemArg,
4469        ret: Location,
4470        need_check: bool,
4471        imported_memories: bool,
4472        offset: i32,
4473        heap_access_oob: Label,
4474        unaligned_atomic: Label,
4475    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4476        self.memory_op(
4477            target,
4478            memarg,
4479            true,
4480            4,
4481            need_check,
4482            imported_memories,
4483            offset,
4484            heap_access_oob,
4485            unaligned_atomic,
4486            |this, addr| {
4487                let mut temps = vec![];
4488                let tmp = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
4489                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
4490                })?;
4491                let dst =
4492                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4493                let org =
4494                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, new, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4495                let reread = this.get_label();
4496                let nosame = this.get_label();
4497
4498                this.emit_label(reread)?;
4499                this.assembler
4500                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S32, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
4501                this.emit_relaxed_cmp(Size::S32, dst, cmp)?;
4502                this.assembler.emit_bcond_label(Condition::Ne, nosame)?;
4503                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
4504                    Size::S32,
4505                    Location::GPR(tmp),
4506                    org,
4507                    Location::GPR(addr),
4508                )?;
4509                this.assembler
4510                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), reread)?;
4511                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
4512
4513                this.emit_label(nosame)?;
4514                if dst != ret {
4515                    this.move_location(Size::S32, ret, dst)?;
4516                }
4517                for r in temps {
4518                    this.release_gpr(r);
4519                }
4520                this.release_gpr(tmp);
4521                Ok(())
4522            },
4523        )
4524    }

4652    fn emit_call_with_reloc(
4653        &mut self,
4654        _calling_convention: CallingConvention,
4655        reloc_target: RelocationTarget,
4656    ) -> Result<Vec<Relocation>, CompileError> {
4657        let mut relocations = vec![];
4658        let next = self.get_label();
4659        let reloc_at = self.assembler.get_offset().0;
4660        self.emit_label(next)?; // this is to be sure the current imm26 value is 0
4661        self.assembler.emit_call_label(next)?;
4662        relocations.push(Relocation {
4663            kind: RelocationKind::Arm64Call,
4664            reloc_target,
4665            offset: reloc_at as u32,
4666            addend: 0,
4667        });
4668        Ok(relocations)
4669    }

4682            ret,

4684        )

4701    fn emit_binop_mul64(

4716    fn emit_binop_udiv64(
4717        &mut self,
4718        loc_a: Location,
4719        loc_b: Location,
4720        ret: Location,
4721        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
4722    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
4723        let mut temps = vec![];
4724        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4725        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4726        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4727
4728        self.assembler
4729            .emit_cbz_label(Size::S64, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
4730        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
4731        self.assembler.emit_udiv(Size::S64, src1, src2, dest)?;
4732        if ret != dest {
4733            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
4734        }
4735        for r in temps {
4736            self.release_gpr(r);
4737        }
4738        Ok(offset)
4739    }
4740    fn emit_binop_sdiv64(
4741        &mut self,
4742        loc_a: Location,
4743        loc_b: Location,
4744        ret: Location,
4745        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
4746        integer_overflow: Label,
4747    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
4748        let mut temps = vec![];
4749        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4750        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4751        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4752
4753        self.assembler
4754            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S64, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
4755        let label_nooverflow = self.assembler.get_label();
4756        let tmp = self.location_to_reg(
4757            Size::S64,
4758            Location::Imm64(0x8000000000000000),
4759            &mut temps,
4760            ImmType::None,
4761            true,
4762            None,
4763        )?;
4764        self.assembler.emit_cmp(Size::S64, tmp, src1)?;
4765        self.assembler
4766            .emit_bcond_label(Condition::Ne, label_nooverflow)?;
4767        self.assembler.emit_movn(Size::S64, tmp, 0)?;
4768        self.assembler.emit_cmp(Size::S64, tmp, src2)?;
4769        self.assembler
4770            .emit_bcond_label_far(Condition::Eq, integer_overflow)?;
4771        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
4772        self.assembler.emit_label(label_nooverflow)?;
4773        self.assembler.emit_sdiv(Size::S64, src1, src2, dest)?;
4774        if ret != dest {
4775            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
4776        }
4777        for r in temps {
4778            self.release_gpr(r);
4779        }
4780        Ok(offset)
4781    }
4782    fn emit_binop_urem64(
4783        &mut self,
4784        loc_a: Location,
4785        loc_b: Location,
4786        ret: Location,
4787        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
4788    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
4789        let mut temps = vec![];
4790        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4791        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4792        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4793        let dest = if dest == src1 || dest == src2 {
4794            let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
4795                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
4796            })?;
4797            temps.push(tmp);
4798            self.assembler
4799                .emit_mov(Size::S32, dest, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
4800            Location::GPR(tmp)
4801        } else {
4802            dest
4803        };
4804        self.assembler
4805            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S64, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
4806        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
4807        self.assembler.emit_udiv(Size::S64, src1, src2, dest)?;
4808        // unsigned remainder : src1 - (src1/src2)*src2
4809        self.assembler
4810            .emit_msub(Size::S64, dest, src2, src1, dest)?;
4811        if ret != dest {
4812            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
4813        }
4814        for r in temps {
4815            self.release_gpr(r);
4816        }
4817        Ok(offset)
4818    }
4819    fn emit_binop_srem64(
4820        &mut self,
4821        loc_a: Location,
4822        loc_b: Location,
4823        ret: Location,
4824        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
4825    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
4826        let mut temps = vec![];
4827        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4828        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4829        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4830        let dest = if dest == src1 || dest == src2 {
4831            let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
4832                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
4833            })?;
4834            temps.push(tmp);
4835            self.assembler
4836                .emit_mov(Size::S64, dest, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
4837            Location::GPR(tmp)
4838        } else {
4839            dest
4840        };
4841        self.assembler
4842            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S64, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
4843        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
4844        self.assembler.emit_sdiv(Size::S64, src1, src2, dest)?;
4845        // unsigned remainder : src1 - (src1/src2)*src2
4846        self.assembler
4847            .emit_msub(Size::S64, dest, src2, src1, dest)?;
4848        if ret != dest {
4849            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
4850        }
4851        for r in temps {
4852            self.release_gpr(r);
4853        }
4854        Ok(offset)
4855    }

4901    fn i64_cmp_ge_s(

4909    fn i64_cmp_gt_s(
4910        &mut self,
4911        loc_a: Location,
4912        loc_b: Location,
4913        ret: Location,
4914    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4915        self.emit_cmpop_i64_dynamic_b(Condition::Gt, loc_a, loc_b, ret)

4981    fn i64_clz(&mut self, src: Location, dst: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4982        self.emit_relaxed_binop(Assembler::emit_clz, Size::S64, src, dst, true)
4983    }
4984    fn i64_ctz(&mut self, src: Location, dst: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4985        let mut temps = vec![];
4986        let src = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, src, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4987        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, dst, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4988        self.assembler.emit_rbit(Size::S64, src, dest)?;
4989        self.assembler.emit_clz(Size::S64, dest, dest)?;
4990        if dst != dest {
4991            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, dst)?;
4992        }
4993        for r in temps {
4994            self.release_gpr(r);
4995        }
4996        Ok(())
4997    }
4998    fn i64_popcnt(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4999        if self.has_neon {
5000            let mut temps = vec![];
5001
5002            let src_gpr =
5003                self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
5004            let dst_gpr =
5005                self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
5006
5007            let mut neon_temps = vec![];
5008            let neon_temp = self.acquire_temp_simd().ok_or_else(|| {
5009                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5010            })?;
5011            neon_temps.push(neon_temp);
5012
5013            self.assembler
5014                .emit_fmov(Size::S64, src_gpr, Size::S64, Location::SIMD(neon_temp))?;
5015            self.assembler.emit_cnt(neon_temp, neon_temp)?;
5016            self.assembler.emit_addv(neon_temp, neon_temp)?;
5017            self.assembler
5018                .emit_fmov(Size::S64, Location::SIMD(neon_temp), Size::S64, dst_gpr)?;
5019
5020            if ret != dst_gpr {
5021                self.move_location(Size::S64, dst_gpr, ret)?;
5022            }
5023
5024            for r in temps {
5025                self.release_gpr(r);
5026            }
5027
5028            for r in neon_temps {
5029                self.release_simd(r);
5030            }
5031        } else {
5032            let mut temps = vec![];
5033            let src =
5034                self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
5035            let dest =
5036                self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
5037            let src = if src == loc {
5038                let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
5039                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5040                })?;
5041                temps.push(tmp);
5042                self.assembler
5043                    .emit_mov(Size::S64, src, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
5044                Location::GPR(tmp)
5045            } else {
5046                src
5047            };
5048            let tmp = {
5049                let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
5050                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5051                })?;
5052                temps.push(tmp);
5053                Location::GPR(tmp)
5054            };
5055            let label_loop = self.assembler.get_label();
5056            let label_exit = self.assembler.get_label();
5057            self.assembler
5058                .emit_mov(Size::S32, Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp), dest)?; // dest <= 0
5059            self.assembler.emit_cbz_label(Size::S64, src, label_exit)?; // src == 0, then goto label_exit
5060            self.assembler.emit_label(label_loop)?;
5061            self.assembler
5062                .emit_add(Size::S32, dest, Location::Imm8(1), dest)?; // dest += 1
5063            self.assembler.emit_clz(Size::S64, src, tmp)?; // clz src => tmp
5064            self.assembler.emit_lsl(Size::S64, src, tmp, src)?; // src << tmp => src
5065            self.assembler
5066                .emit_lsl(Size::S64, src, Location::Imm8(1), src)?; // src << 1 => src
5067            self.assembler.emit_cbnz_label(Size::S64, src, label_loop)?; // src != 0, then goto label_loop
5068            self.assembler.emit_label(label_exit)?;
5069            if ret != dest {
5070                self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
5071            }
5072            for r in temps {
5073                self.release_gpr(r);
5074            }
5075        }
5076
5077        Ok(())
5078    }
5079    fn i64_shl(

5124    fn i64_rol(
5125        &mut self,
5126        loc_a: Location,
5127        loc_b: Location,
5128        ret: Location,
5129    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
5130        // there is no ROL on ARM64. We use ROR with 64-value instead
5131        let mut temps = vec![];
5132        let src2 = match loc_b {
5133            Location::Imm8(imm) => Location::Imm8(64 - (imm & 63)),
5134            Location::Imm32(imm) => Location::Imm8(64 - (imm & 63) as u8),
5135            Location::Imm64(imm) => Location::Imm8(64 - (imm & 63) as u8),
5136            _ => {
5137                let tmp1 = self.location_to_reg(
5138                    Size::S64,
5139                    Location::Imm32(64),
5140                    &mut temps,
5141                    ImmType::None,
5142                    true,
5143                    None,
5144                )?;
5145                let tmp2 =
5146                    self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
5147                self.assembler.emit_sub(Size::S64, tmp1, tmp2, tmp1)?;
5148                tmp1
5149            }
5150        };
5151        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
5152            Assembler::emit_ror,
5153            Size::S64,
5154            loc_a,
5155            src2,
5156            ret,
5157            ImmType::Shift64No0,
5158        )?;
5159        for r in temps {
5160            self.release_gpr(r);
5161        }
5162        Ok(())
5163    }
5164    fn i64_ror(
5165        &mut self,
5166        loc_a: Location,
5167        loc_b: Location,
5168        ret: Location,
5169    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
5170        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
5171            Assembler::emit_ror,
5172            Size::S64,
5173            loc_a,
5174            loc_b,
5175            ret,
5176            ImmType::Shift64No0,
5177        )
5178    }

5201        )

5585            |this, addr| this.emit_relaxed_str8(target_value, Location::Memory(addr, 0)),
5586        )?;
5587        self.assembler.emit_dmb()
5588    }

5639    // i64 atomic Add with i64
5640    fn i64_atomic_add(
5641        &mut self,
5642        loc: Location,
5643        target: Location,
5644        memarg: &MemArg,
5645        ret: Location,
5646        need_check: bool,
5647        imported_memories: bool,
5648        offset: i32,
5649        heap_access_oob: Label,
5650        unaligned_atomic: Label,
5651    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
5652        self.memory_op(
5653            target,
5654            memarg,
5655            true,
5656            8,
5657            need_check,
5658            imported_memories,
5659            offset,
5660            heap_access_oob,
5661            unaligned_atomic,
5662            |this, addr| {
5663                let mut temps = vec![];
5664                let tmp1 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
5665                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5666                })?;
5667                let tmp2 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
5668                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5669                })?;
5670                let dst =
5671                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
5672                let reread = this.get_label();
5673
5674                this.emit_label(reread)?;
5675                this.assembler
5676                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S64, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
5677                this.emit_binop_add64(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
5678                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
5679                    Size::S64,
5680                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
5681                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
5682                    Location::GPR(addr),
5683                )?;
5684                this.assembler
5685                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
5686                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
5687
5688                if dst != ret {
5689                    this.move_location(Size::S64, ret, dst)?;
5690                }
5691                for r in temps {
5692                    this.release_gpr(r);
5693                }
5694                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
5695                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
5696                Ok(())
5697            },
5698        )
5699    }

6226                this.emit_binop_and64(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
6227                this.assembler.emit_stlxrb(
6228                    Size::S64,
6229                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
6230                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
6231                    Location::GPR(addr),
6232                )?;
6233                this.assembler
6234                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
6235                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
6236
6237                if dst != ret {
6238                    this.move_location(Size::S64, ret, dst)?;
6239                }
6240                for r in temps {
6241                    this.release_gpr(r);
6242                }
6243                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
6244                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
6245                Ok(())
6246            },
6247        )
6248    }
6249    // i64 atomic And with u16
6250    fn i64_atomic_and_16u(
6251        &mut self,
6252        loc: Location,
6253        target: Location,
6254        memarg: &MemArg,
6255        ret: Location,
6256        need_check: bool,
6257        imported_memories: bool,
6258        offset: i32,
6259        heap_access_oob: Label,
6260        unaligned_atomic: Label,
6261    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
6262        self.memory_op(
6263            target,
6264            memarg,
6265            true,
6266            2,
6267            need_check,
6268            imported_memories,
6269            offset,
6270            heap_access_oob,
6271            unaligned_atomic,
6272            |this, addr| {
6273                let mut temps = vec![];
6274                let tmp1 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
6275                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
6276                })?;
6277                let tmp2 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
6278                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
6279                })?;
6280                let dst =
6281                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
6282                let reread = this.get_label();
6283
6284                this.emit_label(reread)?;
6285                this.assembler
6286                    .emit_ldaxrh(Size::S64, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
6287                this.emit_binop_and64(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
6288                this.assembler.emit_stlxrh(
6289                    Size::S64,
6290                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
6291                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
6292                    Location::GPR(addr),
6293                )?;
6294                this.assembler
6295                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
6296                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;

6298                if dst != ret {
6299                    this.move_location(Size::S64, ret, dst)?;
6300                }

6868        offset: i32,
6869        heap_access_oob: Label,
6870        unaligned_atomic: Label,
6871    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
6872        self.memory_op(
6873            target,
6874            memarg,
6875            true,
6876            8,
6877            need_check,
6878            imported_memories,
6879            offset,
6880            heap_access_oob,
6881            unaligned_atomic,
6882            |this, addr| {
6883                let mut temps = vec![];
6884                let tmp = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
6885                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
6886                })?;
6887                let dst =
6888                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
6889                let org =
6890                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
6891                let reread = this.get_label();
6892
6893                this.emit_label(reread)?;
6894                this.assembler
6895                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S64, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
6896                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
6897                    Size::S64,
6898                    Location::GPR(tmp),
6899                    org,
6900                    Location::GPR(addr),
6901                )?;
6902                this.assembler
6903                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), reread)?;
6904                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
6905
6906                if dst != ret {
6907                    this.move_location(Size::S64, ret, dst)?;
6908                }
6909                for r in temps {
6910                    this.release_gpr(r);
6911                }
6912                this.release_gpr(tmp);
6913                Ok(())
6914            },
6915        )
6916    }

7091    // i64 atomic Exchange with i64
7092    fn i64_atomic_cmpxchg(
7093        &mut self,
7094        new: Location,
7095        cmp: Location,
7096        target: Location,
7097        memarg: &MemArg,
7098        ret: Location,
7099        need_check: bool,
7100        imported_memories: bool,
7101        offset: i32,
7102        heap_access_oob: Label,
7103        unaligned_atomic: Label,
7104    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7105        self.memory_op(
7106            target,
7107            memarg,
7108            true,
7109            8,
7110            need_check,
7111            imported_memories,
7112            offset,
7113            heap_access_oob,
7114            unaligned_atomic,
7115            |this, addr| {
7116                let mut temps = vec![];
7117                let tmp = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
7118                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
7119                })?;
7120                let dst =
7121                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
7122                let org =
7123                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, new, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
7124                let reread = this.get_label();
7125                let nosame = this.get_label();
7126
7127                this.emit_label(reread)?;
7128                this.assembler
7129                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S64, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
7130                this.emit_relaxed_cmp(Size::S64, dst, cmp)?;
7131                this.assembler.emit_bcond_label(Condition::Ne, nosame)?;
7132                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
7133                    Size::S64,
7134                    Location::GPR(tmp),
7135                    org,
7136                    Location::GPR(addr),
7137                )?;
7138                this.assembler
7139                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), reread)?;
7140                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
7141
7142                this.emit_label(nosame)?;
7143                if dst != ret {
7144                    this.move_location(Size::S64, ret, dst)?;
7145                }
7146                for r in temps {
7147                    this.release_gpr(r);
7148                }
7149                this.release_gpr(tmp);
7150                Ok(())
7151            },
7152        )
7153    }

7344    fn f32_load(
7345        &mut self,
7346        addr: Location,
7347        memarg: &MemArg,
7348        ret: Location,
7349        need_check: bool,
7350        imported_memories: bool,
7351        offset: i32,
7352        heap_access_oob: Label,
7353        unaligned_atomic: Label,
7354    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7355        self.memory_op(
7356            addr,
7357            memarg,
7358            false,
7359            4,
7360            need_check,
7361            imported_memories,
7362            offset,
7363            heap_access_oob,
7364            unaligned_atomic,
7365            |this, addr| this.emit_relaxed_ldr32(Size::S32, ret, Location::Memory(addr, 0)),
7366        )
7367    }
7368    fn f32_save(
7369        &mut self,
7370        target_value: Location,
7371        memarg: &MemArg,
7372        target_addr: Location,
7373        canonicalize: bool,
7374        need_check: bool,
7375        imported_memories: bool,
7376        offset: i32,
7377        heap_access_oob: Label,
7378        unaligned_atomic: Label,
7379    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7380        let canonicalize = canonicalize && self.arch_supports_canonicalize_nan();
7381        self.memory_op(
7382            target_addr,
7383            memarg,
7384            false,
7385            4,
7386            need_check,
7387            imported_memories,
7388            offset,
7389            heap_access_oob,
7390            unaligned_atomic,
7391            |this, addr| {
7392                if !canonicalize {
7393                    this.emit_relaxed_str32(target_value, Location::Memory(addr, 0))
7394                } else {
7395                    this.canonicalize_nan(Size::S32, target_value, Location::Memory(addr, 0))
7396                }
7397            },
7398        )
7399    }

7456
7457    fn convert_f64_i64(
7458        &mut self,
7459        loc: Location,
7460        signed: bool,
7461        ret: Location,
7462    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7463        let mut gprs = vec![];
7464        let mut neons = vec![];
7465        let src = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc, &mut gprs, ImmType::NoneXzr, true, None)?;
7466        let dest = self.location_to_neon(Size::S64, ret, &mut neons, ImmType::None, false)?;
7467        if signed {
7468            self.assembler.emit_scvtf(Size::S64, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7469        } else {
7470            self.assembler.emit_ucvtf(Size::S64, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7471        }
7472        if ret != dest {
7473            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
7474        }
7475        for r in gprs {
7476            self.release_gpr(r);
7477        }
7478        for r in neons {
7479            self.release_simd(r);
7480        }
7481        Ok(())
7482    }
7483    fn convert_f64_i32(
7484        &mut self,
7485        loc: Location,
7486        signed: bool,
7487        ret: Location,
7488    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7489        let mut gprs = vec![];
7490        let mut neons = vec![];
7491        let src = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc, &mut gprs, ImmType::NoneXzr, true, None)?;
7492        let dest = self.location_to_neon(Size::S64, ret, &mut neons, ImmType::None, false)?;
7493        if signed {
7494            self.assembler.emit_scvtf(Size::S32, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7495        } else {
7496            self.assembler.emit_ucvtf(Size::S32, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7497        }
7498        if ret != dest {
7499            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
7500        }
7501        for r in gprs {
7502            self.release_gpr(r);
7503        }
7504        for r in neons {
7505            self.release_simd(r);
7506        }
7507        Ok(())
7508    }
7509    fn convert_f32_i64(
7510        &mut self,
7511        loc: Location,
7512        signed: bool,
7513        ret: Location,
7514    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7515        let mut gprs = vec![];
7516        let mut neons = vec![];
7517        let src = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc, &mut gprs, ImmType::NoneXzr, true, None)?;
7518        let dest = self.location_to_neon(Size::S32, ret, &mut neons, ImmType::None, false)?;
7519        if signed {
7520            self.assembler.emit_scvtf(Size::S64, src, Size::S32, dest)?;
7521        } else {
7522            self.assembler.emit_ucvtf(Size::S64, src, Size::S32, dest)?;
7523        }
7524        if ret != dest {
7525            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
7526        }
7527        for r in gprs {
7528            self.release_gpr(r);
7529        }
7530        for r in neons {
7531            self.release_simd(r);
7532        }
7533        Ok(())
7534    }
7535    fn convert_f32_i32(
7536        &mut self,
7537        loc: Location,
7538        signed: bool,
7539        ret: Location,
7540    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7541        let mut gprs = vec![];
7542        let mut neons = vec![];
7543        let src = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc, &mut gprs, ImmType::NoneXzr, true, None)?;
7544        let dest = self.location_to_neon(Size::S32, ret, &mut neons, ImmType::None, false)?;
7545        if signed {
7546            self.assembler.emit_scvtf(Size::S32, src, Size::S32, dest)?;
7547        } else {
7548            self.assembler.emit_ucvtf(Size::S32, src, Size::S32, dest)?;
7549        }
7550        if ret != dest {
7551            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
7552        }
7553        for r in gprs {
7554            self.release_gpr(r);
7555        }
7556        for r in neons {
7557            self.release_simd(r);
7558        }
7559        Ok(())
7560    }
7561    fn convert_i64_f64(
7562        &mut self,
7563        loc: Location,
7564        ret: Location,
7565        signed: bool,
7566        sat: bool,
7567    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7568        let mut gprs = vec![];
7569        let mut neons = vec![];
7570        let src = self.location_to_neon(Size::S64, loc, &mut neons, ImmType::None, true)?;
7571        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut gprs, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
7572        let old_fpcr = if !sat {
7573            self.reset_exception_fpsr()?;
7574            self.set_trap_enabled(&mut gprs)?
7575        } else {
7576            GPR::XzrSp
7577        };
7578        if signed {
7579            self.assembler
7580                .emit_fcvtzs(Size::S64, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7581        } else {
7582            self.assembler
7583                .emit_fcvtzu(Size::S64, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7584        }
7585        if !sat {
7586            self.trap_float_convertion_errors(old_fpcr, Size::S64, src, &mut gprs)?;
7587        }
7588        if ret != dest {
7589            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
7590        }
7591        for r in gprs {
7592            self.release_gpr(r);
7593        }
7594        for r in neons {
7595            self.release_simd(r);
7596        }
7597        Ok(())
7598    }

7713    fn convert_f64_f32(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7714        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcvt, Size::S32, loc, ret, true)
7715    }
7716    fn convert_f32_f64(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7717        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcvt, Size::S64, loc, ret, true)
7718    }
7719    fn f64_neg(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7720        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fneg, Size::S64, loc, ret, true)
7721    }
7722    fn f64_abs(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7723        let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
7724            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
7725        })?;
7726
7727        self.move_location(Size::S64, loc, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
7728        self.assembler.emit_and(
7729            Size::S64,
7730            Location::GPR(tmp),
7731            Location::Imm64(0x7fffffffffffffffu64),
7732            Location::GPR(tmp),
7733        )?;
7734        self.move_location(Size::S64, Location::GPR(tmp), ret)?;
7735
7736        self.release_gpr(tmp);
7737        Ok(())
7738    }
7739    fn emit_i64_copysign(&mut self, tmp1: GPR, tmp2: GPR) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7740        self.assembler.emit_and(
7741            Size::S64,
7742            Location::GPR(tmp1),
7743            Location::Imm64(0x7fffffffffffffffu64),
7744            Location::GPR(tmp1),
7745        )?;
7746
7747        self.assembler.emit_and(
7748            Size::S64,
7749            Location::GPR(tmp2),
7750            Location::Imm64(0x8000000000000000u64),
7751            Location::GPR(tmp2),
7752        )?;
7753
7754        self.assembler.emit_or(
7755            Size::S64,
7756            Location::GPR(tmp1),
7757            Location::GPR(tmp2),
7758            Location::GPR(tmp1),
7759        )
7760    }
7761    fn f64_sqrt(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7762        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fsqrt, Size::S64, loc, ret, true)
7763    }

7776    fn f64_cmp_ge(
7777        &mut self,
7778        loc_a: Location,
7779        loc_b: Location,
7780        ret: Location,
7781    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7782        let mut temps = vec![];
7783        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
7784        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcmp, Size::S64, loc_b, loc_a, false)?;
7785        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Ls)?;
7786        if ret != dest {
7787            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
7788        }
7789        for r in temps {
7790            self.release_gpr(r);
7791        }
7792        Ok(())
7793    }

7803        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Cc)?;

7805            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;

7807        for r in temps {
7808            self.release_gpr(r);
7809        }
7810        Ok(())
7811    }

7884    fn f64_min(
7885        &mut self,
7886        loc_a: Location,
7887        loc_b: Location,
7888        ret: Location,
7889    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7890        let mut temps = vec![];
7891        let old_fpcr = self.set_default_nan(&mut temps)?;
7892        self.emit_relaxed_binop3_neon(
7893            Assembler::emit_fmin,
7894            Size::S64,
7895            loc_a,
7896            loc_b,
7897            ret,
7898            ImmType::None,
7899        )?;
7900        self.restore_fpcr(old_fpcr)?;
7901        for r in temps {
7902            self.release_gpr(r);
7903        }
7904        Ok(())
7905    }

8084        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
8085        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcmp, Size::S32, loc_a, loc_b, false)?;
8086        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Ls)?;
8087        if ret != dest {
8088            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
8089        }
8090        for r in temps {
8091            self.release_gpr(r);
8092        }
8093        Ok(())
8094    }
8095    fn f32_cmp_lt(
8096        &mut self,
8097        loc_a: Location,
8098        loc_b: Location,
8099        ret: Location,
8100    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8101        let mut temps = vec![];
8102        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
8103        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcmp, Size::S32, loc_a, loc_b, false)?;
8104        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Cc)?;
8105        if ret != dest {
8106            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
8107        }
8108        for r in temps {
8109            self.release_gpr(r);
8110        }
8111        Ok(())
8112    }
8113    fn f32_cmp_ne(
8114        &mut self,
8115        loc_a: Location,
8116        loc_b: Location,
8117        ret: Location,
8118    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8119        let mut temps = vec![];
8120        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
8121        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcmp, Size::S32, loc_a, loc_b, false)?;
8122        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Ne)?;
8123        if ret != dest {
8124            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
8125        }
8126        for r in temps {
8127            self.release_gpr(r);
8128        }
8129        Ok(())
8130    }
8131    fn f32_cmp_eq(
8132        &mut self,
8133        loc_a: Location,
8134        loc_b: Location,
8135        ret: Location,
8136    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8137        let mut temps = vec![];
8138        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
8139        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcmp, Size::S32, loc_a, loc_b, false)?;
8140        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Eq)?;
8141        if ret != dest {
8142            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
8143        }
8144        for r in temps {
8145            self.release_gpr(r);
8146        }
8147        Ok(())
8148    }
8149    fn f32_min(
8150        &mut self,
8151        loc_a: Location,
8152        loc_b: Location,
8153        ret: Location,
8154    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8155        let mut temps = vec![];
8156        let old_fpcr = self.set_default_nan(&mut temps)?;
8157        self.emit_relaxed_binop3_neon(
8158            Assembler::emit_fmin,
8159            Size::S32,
8160            loc_a,
8161            loc_b,
8162            ret,
8163            ImmType::None,
8164        )?;
8165        self.restore_fpcr(old_fpcr)?;
8166        for r in temps {
8167            self.release_gpr(r);
8168        }
8169        Ok(())
8170    }
8171    fn f32_max(
8172        &mut self,
8173        loc_a: Location,
8174        loc_b: Location,
8175        ret: Location,
8176    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8177        let mut temps = vec![];
8178        let old_fpcr = self.set_default_nan(&mut temps)?;
8179        self.emit_relaxed_binop3_neon(
8180            Assembler::emit_fmax,
8181            Size::S32,
8182            loc_a,
8183            loc_b,
8184            ret,
8185            ImmType::None,
8186        )?;
8187        self.restore_fpcr(old_fpcr)?;
8188        for r in temps {
8189            self.release_gpr(r);
8190        }
8191        Ok(())
8192    }

8270    // Singlepass calls import functions through a trampoline.

8279    }
8280    #[cfg(feature = "unwind")]
8281    fn gen_dwarf_unwind_info(&mut self, code_len: usize) -> Option<UnwindInstructions> {
8282        let mut instructions = vec![];
8283        for &(instruction_offset, ref inst) in &self.unwind_ops {
8284            let instruction_offset = instruction_offset as u32;
8285            match *inst {
8286                UnwindOps::PushFP { up_to_sp } => {
8287                    instructions.push((
8288                        instruction_offset,
8289                        CallFrameInstruction::CfaOffset(up_to_sp as i32),
8290                    ));
8291                    instructions.push((
8292                        instruction_offset,
8293                        CallFrameInstruction::Offset(AArch64::X29, -(up_to_sp as i32)),
8294                    ));
8295                }
8296                UnwindOps::Push2Regs {
8297                    reg1,
8298                    reg2,
8299                    up_to_sp,
8300                } => {
8301                    instructions.push((
8302                        instruction_offset,
8303                        CallFrameInstruction::CfaOffset(up_to_sp as i32),
8304                    ));
8305                    instructions.push((
8306                        instruction_offset,
8307                        CallFrameInstruction::Offset(reg2.dwarf_index(), -(up_to_sp as i32) + 8),
8308                    ));
8309                    instructions.push((
8310                        instruction_offset,
8311                        CallFrameInstruction::Offset(reg1.dwarf_index(), -(up_to_sp as i32)),
8312                    ));
8313                }
8314                UnwindOps::DefineNewFrame => {
8315                    instructions.push((
8316                        instruction_offset,
8317                        CallFrameInstruction::CfaRegister(AArch64::X29),
8318                    ));
8319                }
8320                UnwindOps::SaveRegister { reg, bp_neg_offset } => instructions.push((
8321                    instruction_offset,
8322                    CallFrameInstruction::Offset(reg.dwarf_index(), -bp_neg_offset),
8323                )),
8324            }
8325        }
8326        Some(UnwindInstructions {
8327            instructions,
8328            len: code_len as u32,
8329        })
8330    }
8331    #[cfg(not(feature = "unwind"))]
8332    fn gen_dwarf_unwind_info(&mut self, _code_len: usize) -> Option<UnwindInstructions> {
8333        None
8334    }
8335
8336    fn gen_windows_unwind_info(&mut self, _code_len: usize) -> Option<Vec<u8>> {
8337        None
8338    }
8339}

8632    fn tests_arm64() -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8633        let mut machine = MachineARM64::new(None);
8634
8635        test_move_location(&mut machine, Size::S32)?;
8636        test_move_location(&mut machine, Size::S64)?;
8637        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, false, Size::S8)?;
8638        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, false, Size::S16)?;
8639        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, false, Size::S32)?;
8640        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, true, Size::S8)?;
8641        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, true, Size::S16)?;
8642        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, true, Size::S32)?;
8643        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_add32)?;
8644        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_add64)?;
8645        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_sub32)?;
8646        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_sub64)?;
8647        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_and32)?;
8648        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_and64)?;
8649        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_xor32)?;
8650        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_xor64)?;
8651        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_or32)?;
8652        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_or64)?;
8653        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_mul32)?;
8654        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_mul64)?;
8655        test_float_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_add)?;
8656        test_float_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_sub)?;
8657        test_float_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_mul)?;
8658        test_float_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_div)?;
8659        test_float_cmp_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_cmp_eq)?;
8660        test_float_cmp_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_cmp_lt)?;
8661        test_float_cmp_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_cmp_le)?;
8662
8663        Ok(())
8664    }
